Public Telegram

The following telegram from Xi'an is addressed to all newspaper offices: Shaanxi Province has suffered three years of drought and famine, and the number of deaths is countless. The disaster is unprecedented. We are grateful that the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee resolved to issue public bonds of 8 million yuan to help relieve the victims. Everyone is celebrating and hoping for a new life. However, several months have passed, and this has not been realized. We anxiously await a telegram and are even more eager for rescue. After repeated appeals from various parties, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek fortunately approved the issuance of 500,000 yuan. Although this can temporarily relieve the urgent needs, it is ultimately a drop in the bucket. Recently, we received a telegram from Hao Mengjiu, the representative of our province's relief association stationed in Nanjing, stating that there is a rumor that the remaining 300,000 yuan of the above-mentioned allocation will be reallocated to the four provinces of Shaanxi, Gansu, Qinghai, and Ningxia. Upon hearing this, we were shocked and horrified. Because this is the time when the disaster is becoming more and more serious, and if relief is not provided urgently, there will be no chance of survival for the remaining people in Shaanxi. In addition to directly telegramming Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, ordering the full amount to be issued as originally planned to maintain credibility, we humbly appeal in this telegram, hoping that you will have compassion for the extreme disaster in Shaanxi and quickly send a telegram to the central government, asking them to quickly investigate and clarify. If there is an agreement on the above-mentioned reallocation, please cancel it immediately and complete the relief effort to the end. We will be grateful for your kindness forever. We eagerly await your reply. Yang Hucheng, Chairman of the Shaanxi Provincial Government, signed with winter seal.

Important News

After Xu Yuanquan Returned to Sha City from Hankou 2

Supervising the Suppression of He Long's Remnants and Other Red Bandits

Military Affairs in Western Hubei Are All Under the Command of Xu

Hankou Correspondence: Xu Yuanquan, the commissioner for bandit suppression and rural pacification in Sichuan, Hunan, and Hubei, previously came to Hankou from Shashi to pay respects to He Chengjun, the head of the Wuhan Pacification Headquarters. He reported on the progress of bandit suppression in western Hubei and requested instructions. The headquarters, noting Xu's arrival in Hankou, intended to convene a conference in Wuhan with various generals stationed in Hubei to discuss the pacification of the province. However, Xu believed that He Long's remnant bandits were causing disturbances in Badong, Zigui, and Xingshan counties, and for the sake of thorough annihilation, it was inconvenient for him to stay in Hankou for long. Therefore, the conference did not take place. On the morning of the 14th at 8:00 AM, he returned to Shashi by civilian airline to resume his duties. His staff traveled west on the Wugua merchant ship. After arriving in Shashi, Xu immediately supervised his troops and launched an offensive against the bandit strongholds in Xingshan. He also joined forces with Zhang Ying, Jue, Wang Lingji, and Guo Xun's divisions to encircle and suppress the bandits. The bandit disasters in various counties of western Hubei were severe. Xu consulted with the Civil Affairs Department and the Relief Committee of the provincial government to distribute emergency relief. In the future, Xu will assess the severity of the situation in each area and allocate aid accordingly. As for the local government affairs in each county, the Wuhan Pacification Headquarters and the provincial government have decided that Xu will be responsible for command and control during the bandit suppression period. Those who fail to carry out orders effectively will be subject to military law. The provincial government has already issued an order to the magistrates of Mianyang, Jianli, Gong'an, Shishou, Jiangling, Jingmen, and Qianjiang counties to strictly comply. (October 14th)

Second Day of National Assembly Elections in Hankou 3

Hankou Correspondence: The election of representatives to the National Assembly in Hankou continued on the 14th, still divided into fourteen districts and over twenty polling places. The voting groups, in addition to the district farmers' associations (districts one through six), Ruikang Silk Factory Labor Union, Jiji Electric Plant, Glass Industry Labor Union, Dyeing Industry Labor Union, and the Tenth District Wharf Association, which had already completed their voting on the first day, all continued to vote. Furthermore, groups such as the Water Plant Labor Union, Fuxin Factory, and Huai Salt Industry Labor Union, which were scheduled to vote on this day, also participated. The total number of voting citizens was still over 20,000, with larger turnouts in the sixth, tenth, eleventh, and twelfth polling districts. Thanks to the effective maintenance of order by the military and police, the guidance of the instructors, and the supervision of supervisors Liu Wendao and Yang Zaichun, order was strictly maintained in all polling places. Only in the sixth polling place (Xinshi Market) was there another incident of someone being forced to write ballots for others. The person was arrested and taken to the municipal government for strict interrogation. (April 14th)

Hunan Province Discovers Case of Illicit Special Tax Collection 4

Related Officials Have Been Removed from Their Posts and Are Under Investigation

Changsha Correspondence: A major case has recently been discovered in Hunan, involving Guo Tao, the deputy division commander of the 15th Division and concurrently the commander of the Hunan provincial capital's garrison; Wang Hanchuan, the director of the provincial capital's Public Security Bureau; Wang Zhengshi, the magistrate of Changsha County; and Yang Dihua, the captain of the Water Police Corps. These four individuals are accused of unauthorized extra taxation (i.e., opium tax) and dividing the tax money among themselves, amounting to hundreds of thousands of dollars. Special goods entering Hunan from Guizhou are subject to a special tax of 400 yuan per shi, which is collected by the Lianghu Special Tax Clearing Office established by the Ministry of Finance in Baoqing. The collected tax revenue is split, with half going to the central government and half to the Fourth Route Army's military expenses. Monthly tax revenue ranges from over one million yuan to at least 500,000 to 600,000 yuan, making it a major source of income for the province. According to established practice, after paying taxes and affixing stamps in Baoqing, goods can circulate throughout Hunan without being subject to further taxation. However, Guo Tao, Wang Hanchuan, Wang Zhengshi, and Yang Dihua, seeing the potential for profit, colluded to engage in malpractice. They privately collected 20 yuan per shi (some say 40 yuan) on special goods transported to Hankou via Changsha, dividing the money among themselves. This practice has been going on for over half a year without being discovered. The amount of illegally collected tax money totals hundreds of thousands of yuan. Recently, He Jian transferred Cao Sui's 4th Regiment of the 31st Division to garrison Changsha. After Cao's regimental commander discovered the situation, he secretly reported it to Division Commander Tao Guang, who in turn reported everything to He Jian. He Jian dispatched personnel to investigate, and after confirming the facts, he was enraged. In his capacity as the commander-in-chief of the Fourth Route Army, he first removed Guo Tao from his post and placed him under investigation. He also appointed Hu Da as the commander of the provincial capital's garrison and concurrently in charge of the Changsha Fortress. Furthermore, since Wang Hanchuan, Wang Zhengshi, and Yang Dihua were civil officials, he specially requested the provincial government to severely punish them and recover the illegally collected tax money. After the case was discovered, it attracted a great deal of attention in Hunan. The following is a transcript of the Fourth Route Army Headquarters' official letter to the Hunan Provincial Government: "Regarding the matter of requesting instructions, the clearing of special taxes was originally intended to support military needs. The central government established an office to handle this, which was done out of necessity. Our department was ordered to assist and has long issued orders to all agencies prohibiting exceptional taxation that would hinder tax collection. All officials should understand this purpose and strive to assist in order to increase tax revenue and maintain military morale. However, we previously received a report from Division Commander Tao Guang of the 31st Division, based on a report from Regimental Commander Cao Sui, stating that the garrison command was collecting exceptional taxes on special goods passing through the provincial capital. We were greatly surprised and ordered Commander Guo Tao to submit a clear report on the collection situation. Now, Commander Guo's report states that it was purely at the repeated request of merchants and that it was not extortion by his department, the Changsha County Government, the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, or the Water Police Corps. He has submitted a statement of income and expenses, totaling 2,874.40 yuan, requesting review and instructions, along with an attached list of income and expenses. In light of this, and having reviewed the report and attachments, we find that a clear order has been issued to unify the collection of special taxes, and no agency is permitted to arbitrarily impose additional levies. Even in special circumstances, the matter should be reported to the headquarters for approval before proceeding. However, the commander did not report in advance and instead, at the request of merchants, divided the tax money with the Changsha County Public Security Bureau and the Water Police Corps. This is illegal and inexcusable and should be punished to maintain official integrity. In addition to the order already issued to remove him from his post and place him under investigation, the Director of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, Wang Hanchuan, the Magistrate of Changsha County, Wang Zhengshi, and the Captain of the Water Police Corps, Yang Dihua, should also be reported to the Hunan Provincial Government for separate punishment. All collected tax money should be handed over to the headquarters, and the submitted expenses will not be approved. You are hereby notified of this order. The attachments are kept on file and distributed. You are requested to investigate and punish the Director of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, Wang Hanchuan, the Magistrate of Changsha County, Wang Zhengshi, and the Captain of the Water Police Corps, Yang Dihua, separately, and to order them to recover the tax money they received in full to maintain official integrity and prioritize tax collection. Your reply is requested. (December 12th)"

Liaoning Province National Assembly Elections Completed After Extension 5

Shenyang Correspondence: The schedule for the election of Liaoning and Ningxia representatives to the National Assembly was previously shortened by the Provincial Office, and all counties were ordered to submit their voter registration books by the end of March. Subsequently, because the counties failed to submit them on time, the deadline was extended to the 4th of this month. However, Antu, Kangping, Tao'an, and Changbai counties still failed to submit their books by the deadline. The Provincial Office, due to the pressing deadline and the impossibility of waiting any longer, and because the large number of registration books required time for review, decided to slightly change the election schedule. Yesterday, it sent a telegram to the supervisors of each county to inform them. The original telegram stated: "(To be reviewed by the election supervisors of each county: Regarding the matter of shortening the election schedule as decided by this office, a telegram has already been sent ordering compliance. Subsequently, because the registration books to be compiled by each county were not submitted by the end of last month, this office, for the sake of exercising caution in the election, sent another telegram extending the deadline for submission to the 4th of this month. However, the reorganization of various groups takes time, and counties in remote areas also face transportation difficulties, making it difficult to meet the deadline. As of today, Antu, Kangping, Tao'an, and Changbai counties have not yet submitted their books. The deadline is pressing, and it is impossible to wait any longer. Therefore, we have completed the review of the registration books that have been submitted over the past few days, working late into the night. The total number of registered voters in the entire province is over 470,000, making the printing of the master registration book a complex process that cannot be completed on schedule. It is necessary to slightly change the schedule again. The revised dates are listed below: (1) The general supervisor will review the qualifications, create the registration book, and issue a public announcement to the counties, to be completed by April 12th; (2) Voters will submit requests for correction of errors or omissions, and the election supervisors will announce the voting date, to be completed by April 14th; (3) Various groups will vote, and the election supervisors will prepare reports and submit them to the general supervisor, to be completed by April 21st; (4) The general supervisor will calculate the number of votes, determine the elected representatives, and notify the elected representatives, to be completed by April 23rd; (5) The elected representatives will respond to whether or not they wish to be elected, and the general supervisor will issue certificates and travel and expense allowances, to be completed by April 24th. The above revised dates are to be complied with after reporting and issuing a telegram. Do not delay. [Seal of Jia, General Supervisor of the Liaoning and Ningxia Elections], 1."

Jinan City National Assembly Election, First Day

Jinan Correspondence: The National Assembly representative elections in this province are scheduled to take place on the 13th, 14th, and 15th of this month. The first day is for professional groups such as education associations, journalists, lawyers, and doctors; the second day is for industrial groups such as labor unions and chambers of commerce; and the third day is for farmers' associations. Yesterday (the 13th) was the first day. In addition to the various counties and cities starting their elections according to regulations, Jinan City also began its elections. The polling place was located inside the municipal government building, with four ballot boxes set up: one for each of the education association, the journalists' association, the lawyers' association, and the doctors' association. Starting at 7:00 AM, members of the various groups arrived at the polling place to vote. Voting ended at 4:30 PM. Then, the ballots were counted in four groups, and the counting was completed at 10:00 PM. The names of those with the most votes from each group are listed below: (1) He Siyuan, 247 votes (Education Association); (2) Zhang Hongjian, 226 votes (Education Association); (3) Cai Zisheng, 161 votes (Education Association); (4) Zhang Siwei, 155 votes (Lawyers' Association); (5) Liu Cibi, 126 votes (Education Association); (6) He Bingru, 106 votes (Journalists' Association); (7) Wang Fuhui, 93 votes (Doctors' Association); (8) Chai Guanjun, 73 votes (Lawyers' Association); (9) Wang Jinxin, 63 votes (Education Association); (10) Xia Yuxuan, 63 votes (Education Association).

Baodugu Bandits Attempt to Flee Southward but Fail 6

Jinan Correspondence: The bandits led by Sun Meisong in Baodugu, after Han Fuju arrived in Tengxian to supervise the siege, realized they could not escape. They then came up with a wild idea of joining forces with the bandits in Mengshan to flee southward. This was detected by the military, and Han telegraphed Wang Jun, commander of the 7th Division, to send troops to intercept them. Wang immediately dispatched Li Wenbin's brigade and Hu Yanzhi's regiment from north of Xuzhou, joining forces with Chen Chuanwen's regiment (originally stationed in Lincheng and Zaozhuang) to attack them from both sides. Seeing that the situation was hopeless, the Sun bandits fled back to their old nest in Baodugu. Han has ordered all the troops to begin a siege of Baodugu on the 13th. The bandits led by Wang Baichuan in Julinggu near Linqu will also be eliminated soon. The following are the telegrams from Han Fuju reporting the victories: (1) Notice: 1. Your brother [Han Fuju] arrived in Yanzhou on the 10th; 2. The 1st Regiment of the Pistol Brigade arrived in Qufu; the brigade's special service battalion and transportation, heavy artillery, and mortar platoons arrived in Yanzhou on the 10th and will go to Tengxian tomorrow morning (the 11th); 3. The Lunan Militia entered Sishui on the 10th; 4. The Mengshan bandits have been eliminated, and orders have been given to all units to lift the siege of Mengshan and advance on Baodugu; 5. According to a telegram from Division Commander Wang Zhiping (Wang Jun), Sun Meisong's bandits have fled into Yixian, secretly planning with bandits from Mengshan and Huxi to replicate the Lincheng incident by looting trains north of Hanzhuang and south of Guanqiao. Orders have been given to all units and the militias of all counties to strictly guard against Sun's bandits. Sincerely, Han Fuju [seal] on the 10th. (2) Notice: 1. According to a report from Division Commander Chen, the bandit leader Mao Xuetian has led his remnants to Qingshan. Orders have been given to Zhao's brigade to encircle and suppress them. Furthermore, the Lunan Militia stationed in Pingyi has been ordered to proceed to Shangye to block the bandits. 2. Regarding the bandits in Baodugu, orders have been given to all units to advance and encircle them on the 13th. The bandits are currently in a state of panic and are said to be fleeing to Huxi. 3. According to a report from Division Commander Qiao, after Chen's brigade tightly surrounded and attacked the bandits in Julinggu, the bandits fought among themselves over supplies and suffered many casualties from the artillery fire. They will be eliminated within a few days. Sincerely, Han Fuju [seal] on the 12th.

Wang Jun Goes to Yanzhou to Discuss Bandit Suppression 7

And Orders the Railway Protection Troops to Suppress Scattered Bandits

Xuzhou Correspondence: Wang Jun, the commander of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway Garrison, recently received a report from Chen Chuanwen, the regimental commander of the 70th Regiment of the 12th Division, which is participating in the siege of the Baodugu bandits on the Lincheng-Zaozhuang branch line, stating that the bandits may flee west and join forces with the bandits in Huxi. He dispatched Li Wenbin, the commander of the 21st Brigade, to lead Hu Yanzhi's 41st Regiment to Lincheng to intercept them. Now, Wang is going to Yanzhou this morning (the 13th) at 10:00 AM on the Taiping armored train to understand the true situation of the bandits in southern Shandong. Staff Officer Su Ziwen and Adjutant Jin Shuzhi are traveling with him. The 7th Platoon of the 3rd Battalion of the Railway Artillery Brigade stationed in Xuzhou is also departing with Wang. Wang plans to go to Lincheng first to meet with Li Wenbin, and then to Zaozhuang for inspection. The armored train that Wang previously requested to be transferred from Bian has already been led by Jiang Yin, the platoon commander of the 5th Platoon of the 2nd Battalion stationed in Bian, and passed through Xuzhou northward this morning, patrolling the Lincheng-Tengxian line for protection and cooperative suppression. It is also reported that the troops participating in the siege of the Baodugu bandits are very strong. Han Fuju, Ma Hongkui, and Chen Yaohan will also meet with Wang Jun in Yanzhou to discuss the joint suppression plan, in order to completely eliminate the bandit troubles in southern Shandong. Wang is expected to return to Xuzhou in three or four days. Yesterday, Wang Jun also issued an order to all railway protection troops to strictly patrol and engage in guerilla warfare to prevent scattered bandits from fleeing to the Tianjin-Pukou Railway line. The Garrison Command has now issued the following announcement: "It is hereby announced that the Tianjin-Pukou Railway is of utmost importance to transportation. This command is ordered to garrison it and must take strict precautions to maintain railway administration. Now that the troops stationed in various places are actively searching and suppressing the bandits, there is a deep concern that they may cause disturbances. It is specially ordered that all railway protection troops dispatch teams to patrol and engage in guerilla warfare within 50 li on both sides of the railway, closely cooperate with local security forces, and work together to search and suppress bandits in order to eliminate the bandits and prevent disturbances. Detectives should also be dispatched at any time to conduct thorough reconnaissance in nearby villages. If there are any reactionary elements or bandits hiding and causing trouble, the village chiefs and others must immediately report to the troops stationed in various places, who will be responsible for the suppression. Anyone who conceals information or colludes with the bandits will be arrested, verified, and punished according to law. This announcement is hereby issued for the general knowledge of all residents, who must cooperate with the troops stationed in various places to eliminate the bandits and ensure local peace. This is of utmost importance." (April 13th)

Shanxi Provincial Government Maintains Provincial Currency Measures 8

Recommendations from the Financial Reorganization Design Committee

Taiyuan Correspondence: The Shanxi Provincial Government and the Provincial Party Headquarters, the Chamber of Commerce, and others have jointly organized the Financial Reorganization Design Committee. The committee has held meetings for days to discuss ways to maintain the provincial currency. Yesterday, it submitted six proposed measures to the provincial government for adoption. The provincial government has approved them. The measures are as follows: (1) The directors and supervisors of the provincial bank are responsible for announcing the amount of currency issued by the bank and all its assets to the public in detail, and then publishing the bank's currency inflows, outflows, and uses monthly to dispel public doubts. Approved. (2) After the military is reorganized and placed under the command of the deputy commander-in-chief, all military pay will naturally be received and distributed by the deputy commander-in-chief's headquarters. From now on, under no circumstances may military pay be withdrawn from the provincial bank. Approved. Military expenses will be raised through other means and will no longer be withdrawn from the provincial bank. (3) The provincial government will formulate measures to strictly prohibit money shops from engaging in forward exchange transactions and restrict money shops from purchasing or hoarding large amounts of silver dollars. Approved and transferred to the Finance Department to draft measures for discussion. (4) The provincial bank is ordered to make every effort to buy back provincial currency in the money market every day to suppress the exchange rate and prevent it from falling sharply. After buying it back, it should be burned immediately. The provincial bank will be ordered to reply. (5) Strictly investigate the large-scale outflow of silver dollars from the province. When merchants need to transport large amounts of silver dollars out of the province, the Chamber of Commerce will apply to the provincial government for special permission to issue passports. Approved, but procedures for issuing passports must be stipulated. (6) The provincial government will order the Taiyuan City Chamber of Commerce and county governments to instruct all shops and landlords to continue to use provincial currency as the unit of account for prices and rents, and not to set prices in silver dollars separately. The provincial government will negotiate with state-owned institutions to accept provincial currency at market prices. Approved. (April 11th)

Jiangsu Chamber of Commerce 10

Results of Representatives' Petition in Nanjing

The chambers of commerce of various counties in Jiangsu Province believed that the business tax regulations stipulated by the Jiangsu Department of Finance violated the guidelines set by the ministry. They held a meeting in Zhenjiang and elected representatives to petition in Nanjing. Subsequently, although the Ministry of Finance made some revisions to the Jiangsu Province business tax regulations, they still did not fully comply with the ministry's guidelines and had not been reviewed by the Central Political Conference. They held another meeting in Zhenjiang and decided to continue the petition and elected representatives to go to Nanjing for the second time to petition various ministries and departments. Yesterday (the 14th) at 8:30 AM, the representatives from the various county chambers of commerce, including Lu Huan, Yu Xiaochuan, Shen Zhiwan, Qian Sunqing, Cheng Ganqing, Ren Congfu, Li Shengbo, Wang Jingting, Lan Bohua, and Xu Zhuang, arrived in Nanjing. They first went to the Ministry of Industry, where they were received by Section Chief Zhang Yiqiu. The representatives stated the purpose of their petition, saying that the previous petition had received assistance from the ministry, but although the Ministry of Finance had made some revisions to the original regulations, many of them still did not fully comply with the guidelines. Now, the Ministry of Finance has submitted the revised regulations to the Central Political Conference and the Legislative Yuan for review. They cannot be implemented before they are approved, so they requested the ministry's assistance. Section Chief Zhang said that the Ministry of Finance's revision of the Jiangsu Province business tax regulations will be submitted to the Central Political Conference, and Minister Kong of their ministry is a member of the Central Political Conference and will forward the petition to Minister Kong and submit it to the meeting for review. Next, they went to the Ministry of Finance, where they were received by Section Chief Zhou Gangren of the Taxation Department. After the representatives stated their case, Section Chief Zhou said that the Ministry of Finance had submitted the revised regulations to the Legislative Yuan and the Central Political Conference for review and that he would sign the petition and forward it to the minister, who would then forward it to the Central Political Conference and the Legislative Yuan for consideration. Next, they went to the Executive Yuan, where they were received by Secretary Liu Yongkai. After the representatives stated their case, Secretary Liu promised to forward the petition to the Central Political Conference. Next, they went to the Legislative Yuan, where they were received by Secretary Tang Shiwei. In addition to stating the purpose of their petition, the representatives said that national legislation should be trustworthy and credible. If the implementing agencies arbitrarily interpret the articles and expand or contract them at will, it would be a great loss to the purpose of legislation. They requested the Legislative Yuan to specify the contents of this review in detail so that no implementing agency could freely expand or contract them, in order to uphold the spirit of legislation, which would be fortunate for the merchants. Secretary Tang said that he would forward their opinions to the president and adopt them during the review. The representatives then took their leave.

太湖 Giant Bandit 11

Tai Bao Ashu's Confession

The Pacification Office's Reply Approves Execution in Zhangyan

The Jiangsu Pacification Superintendent's Office recently received a telegram from Cao Pang, Commander of the Songhu Pacification Sub-district, stating that Tai Bao Ashu (also known as Xu Tianxiong), the ringleader of the Taihu Pudong gang of bandits captured in Shanghai on the 5th of this month, along with Xu Fusheng, are currently detained in the Minhang Water Police District. Due to repeated requests from the public and organizations in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces for their swift execution to appease public anger, and considering the mountain of accumulated cases and unpardonable crimes committed by the bandit Tai Bao Ashu and his accomplices, the telegram inquired whether it would be appropriate to comply with public sentiment and approve their execution in Zhangyan Town, Jinshan County, requesting instructions for compliance. Superintendent Zhang telegraphed Commander Cao the day before yesterday, approving the execution of the two bandits. The original telegram stated briefly that the captured bandit leaders Tai Bao Ashu and Xu Fusheng had committed heinous crimes and approved the requested action, ordering immediate execution and reporting back for record-keeping. The following is a transcript of Tai Bao Ashu's confession: Xu Tianxiong, also known as Zhengming, or Tai Bao Ashu, 31 years old, from Jinshan County, served as a platoon leader in the newly formed 16th Division 7th Company of the Revolutionary Army and as a joint defense squad leader under Chen Xiongzhou in Lishui. He joined the Communist army on March 8th of the 18th year of the Republic of China, starting his gang in Liujia Yanqiao. At that time, there were only three of us: Wang Amei, also known as Qiming, nicknamed Piggy Girl, and Zhang Tongsheng, also known as Long Legs Pai Si Quan, with about 300 followers, about 10 to 20 guns, including rifles and Mauser pistols. The boats were found outside. In September, introduced by Weng Mingzheng from Jinshan, we joined Yan Huchen, sent by Qu Qiubai of the Red Party, and were appointed as Commander of the Jiangsu Fourth Route Mobile Detachment of the Party Protection and National Salvation Army, carrying out red work and waiting for an opportunity to revolt. Later, due to the interruption of supplies, we could not maintain ourselves and began to rob. However, when we arrived at a place, we initially borrowed from people, and we sometimes encountered troops, but neither side opened fire. It was not because the troops had inside information with us, but because the number of troops that came out was limited, and they knew that their strength was not equal to ours, so they dared not fight with us. We have always adhered to the principle of not offending others unless they offend us, so we were just so-so. I originally had a lot of guns, mostly robbed from Yaqian, Xincang, and Xinmiaogang, totaling about one hundred and several dozen. After the two major battles of Gaoxu and Zhujiahe, they were almost completely lost. The remaining ones were distributed by Zhang Tongsheng, Song Xiqing, Shen Ziqing, etc. (currently committing crimes in the Baili Baitang area). Now there are only 15 rifles, 7 Mauser pistols, and 1 machine gun left. Several guns were confiscated by the Zhejiang Security Team on the 19th day of the first month of the lunar calendar last year. The rest were handed over to my brother Xu Fusheng for safekeeping. I don't know where they are hidden. I also have appointment letters from the Communist Party's Yan Huchen and various places, as well as various counterfeit seals, such as the Commander of the Fourth Route Mobile Detachment of the Party Protection and National Salvation Army, the Commander-in-Chief of the Second Front Army of the Jiangsu Fourth Route of the Army, Navy, and Air Force of the Republic of China, and the Commander of the Songhu Eight Counties Guerrilla Army. I have also appointed many regimental commanders, battalion commanders, and boat captains, and I can't remember them all for a while. I only remember the big ones, such as Deputy Division Commander Wang Qiming, First Regiment Commander Zhang Tongsheng, Second Regiment Commander Wang Youru, Third Regiment Commander Zhao Guomin, Political Department Li Wenjun, Chen Xiongzhou, and Gu Peizhang, battalion commanders Tao Hulong, Pan Musheng, He Yinyu, and more than ten others. The many people listed in the bandit roster were indeed all appointed by me. Speaking of the kidnapping and robbery cases committed in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, we have really done a lot, and there is no need to describe them in detail. Even if I say it, I can't remember clearly, but roughly speaking, there are one thousand several hundred cases. Even the firefights with the police have happened several times. As for the French woman kidnapped at Dianshan Lake and the killing of the Public Security Bureau Chief and the District Head in Lüxiang, I also did it. In short, I can be regarded as a leader among bandits and a strongman of the Communist Party. There is no need to say anything more.

Local Communication

Suzhou

A Private Mail Boat Robbed Mid-Way: A certain private mail boat traveling between Changshu and Suzhou was robbed yesterday morning (the 15th) while sailing through Wuta. Customer accounts and goods were robbed, resulting in significant losses. The mail boat owner has arrived in Suzhou to report to the water and land police teams and request their pursuit.

The Reformatory Will Be Established Soon: The Jiangsu Reformatory, organized by the High Court, has been completed. The date of establishment is June 1st. It is understood that the Director of Education for the Reformatory must be appointed by the Central Party Headquarters. As for the guards, twenty-eight people were selected a few days ago. The selected personnel are scheduled to go to the Third Prison today (the 16th) for training. They will be assigned as guards of the Reformatory when it is established.

Reaction to Stamp Inspection Not Following Scheduled Dates: The Wuxian County Chamber of Commerce previously received a letter from the silk and satin industry association stating that the local stamp tax bureau does not follow the scheduled periods to inspect stamps together with the public security police, thereby causing harassment to merchants and civilians. They requested the chamber of commerce to forward a petition for strict prohibition. After receiving the letter, the Chamber of Commerce immediately petitioned the Ministry of Finance and the Provincial Stamp and Tobacco Tax Bureau to issue a notice to prohibit this, but it was not approved. After receiving the reply, the Chamber of Commerce convened a meeting of representatives from the industry association and resolved to send letters to all county chambers of commerce, unanimously advocating for the continuation of the petition to the Ministry of Finance for instructions.

Scheduled Election of Representatives for National Conference by Agricultural and Educational Circles: The voter registration for the National Conference election in Wuxian County by agricultural, educational, and free professional groups has been received. Voting is scheduled for the 21st and vote counting on the 22nd. 960 members of the Education Association, with Yang Yongqing and Pan Shenming as supervisors. 35 members of the Medical Association, with Gu Zuhan as supervisor. 372 members of various district and township farmers' associations, with Liao Jianan, Fan Boyin, and Qian Jieyi as supervisors.

Wujiang

Another Kidnapping Case Near Beiqi: The home of Ni Cheng-ying, a farmer in Zhuangtianshang, Beiqi District, was broken into by bandits on the night of the 12th. Ornaments were robbed, and his mother and two younger brothers were kidnapped before the bandits leisurely sailed away into Taihu Lake.

Wuxi

Another Case of Illegally Printing Silkworm Seed Qualification Certificates: The Liu Yuanlong Printing Shop outside Guangfu Gate in this city illegally printed silkworm seed qualification certificates. Witnesses have already been handed over to the court for interrogation. Unexpectedly, Sun Zhinan, the owner of the Youyi Zhai Printing Shop under Shengxiang Bridge in the city, also illegally printed 1,400 of these qualification certificates and took them to the home of Sun Zanqing, who sells silkworm seeds, asking him to sell them. As Zanqing was in Shanghai on business and not at home, Sun's mother paid 75 yuan and bought all of them. Zanqing returned home the day before yesterday and realized that they were counterfeit certificates. He immediately turned Sun Zhinan in to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau, and Branch Chief Gao transferred him to the General Bureau, which then transferred him to the County Court. Prosecutor Zhu opened a court for investigation. As a result, the plaintiff was ordered to return, and the defendant was detained pending investigation.

Water Police Privately Settled a Tobacco Case, Referred to District for Investigation: Wang Rude, a policeman from the 9th Team under the 2nd District of the Provincial Public Security Team stationed in Wuxi, confiscated tobacco in Xizhu Lane, Yixing County, the day before yesterday and privately settled the case. The team leader found out and placed Wang Rude under surveillance. At the same time, police officers were dispatched to arrest Zhu Hongpei and Zhu Chongguang, two drug dealers selling narcotics. More than 1,400 red pills, more than ten taels of pill ash, three opium pipes, and a set of mahjong tiles were seized. They were immediately taken to the team, and the team leader opened a court for interrogation. The tobacco offenders confessed to selling and smoking drugs. Yesterday, they were presented to Wuxi and sent to the district office for investigation.

Jiangyin

Conclusion of a House Collapse Fatality: The case of Shi Honglang's house in Shijia Lane, Beiwai, collapsed due to a fire. He was building a house a few days ago when his cousin Shi Ganrong removed the roof supports and damaged the foundation. On the afternoon of the 13th, Qian Shunpei was delivering soil bricks and pushed them into the house, causing a collapse that crushed him to death. Yesterday morning (the 14th), Supervising Officer Wu, along with the coroner, went to inspect the body and confirmed that Qian Shunpei was crushed to death. In the afternoon, Shi Honglang, his sister-in-law Shi Xu, the deceased's father Qian Xiangbao, the water worker Qian Rugen, and the perpetrator Qian Ganrong were interrogated. Shi Xu testified that she saw Ganrong damage the foundation, causing the house to collapse. The deceased's father stated in court that he did not want to pursue the matter. After the interrogation, the water worker Qian Rugen was instructed to compensate the deceased. Ganrong was placed in the custody of bailiffs, and the court adjourned. It was later learned that Ganrong was willing to pay 350 yuan as compensation for funeral expenses to settle the matter.

The Dasheng Bao Newspaper Is About to Be Published: After the Minsheng Shangbao and Jiangyin newspapers ceased publication, only the Chengqing Dangbao and Jiangsheng Bao remained. Recently, Sha Shihe organized the Dasheng Bao, scheduled for publication on the 18th. Fan Dilin founded the Ming Bao three-day journal, which has already been published.

Zhu Zhaokui Was Arrested in Wuxi: Zhu Zhaokui, a former committee member of the Qingchang Township Administrative Bureau in the Eleventh District, was accused by Shen of withholding public funds and remaining salt bonds. He was repeatedly summoned but failed to appear, and was avoiding the matter by staying away. On the 13th, through Jiang's assistance, he was arrested in Wuxi. Yesterday (the 14th), County Magistrate Li ordered the Public Security Bureau to dispatch Inspector Zhang Rongsheng to Wuxi to escort him.

Ji Hehua Was Found Not Guilty of Counter-Revolutionary Activities: Ji Hehua, the former director of the municipal administrative bureau, was sentenced on the 7th by the Provisional Military Tribunal of the province on the same day as Cai Rushan. Cai Rushan was sent back to his original county on the 11th to serve a 15-year prison sentence. Ji Hehua was found not guilty of counter-revolutionary activities and will be released soon. The entire file of the Ji-Cai case has been sent to the High Court, as there are still cases involving Xing Songwen, the former district head of the First District, Assistant Xu Yan, Zhou Qiujiang, a former committee member of the Chamber of Commerce, and Xu Awu, a newspaper deliverer, that have not been investigated. These files must be reviewed before investigation can begin.

Danyang

Party Members Elect National Assembly Representatives: The election of National Assembly representatives by party members of the district branches in this county was held simultaneously on the 10th. Yesterday's vote count showed that Niu Yongjian, Di Ying, Huang Yuren, Zhou Jieren, Ye Xiufeng, Wang Xiaoying, Qi Xiyong, and Yang Xingqin received the most votes. The party and government have jointly reported this to the province.

Argument Between Father and Son Leads to Death: Wang Zibao, a farmer in Xiangcao Village, had three sons. The eldest son, Xiaozhen, was unfilial and addicted to opium. Last night, Zibao advised him with good words, but Xiaozhen responded with vicious words. Zibao was momentarily angered, picked up a stone, and accidentally broke Xiaozhen's forehead, causing brain matter to flow out, resulting in immediate death. The district public office in that area learned of the matter and has sent Wang Zibao to the county government for investigation.

Autopsy Ordered in Murder Case: Zhu Alin from Jiangjia Township, Beixiang, was doing business outside. In December of last year, he returned home with his fellow villager Wei Chuanxiao and others. He died halfway, and his body has already been coffined. His elder brother, Farong, believed that his brother's death was unclear and filed a petition with the county government requesting an autopsy. County Magistrate Shen, upon receiving the petition, deemed the matter related to human life and appointed a supervising officer to conduct an autopsy with the coroner at Dananmen yesterday. The autopsy revealed that the kidneys and testicles were crushed, confirming that he had been murdered. The search for the murderer is underway.

Zhenjiang

The Qingxiang Bureau Orders the Formation of Self-Defense Corps: The Jiangsu Provincial Qingxiang Bureau believes that during the Qingxiang period, self-defense corps should be organized in accordance with the Self-Defense Corps Law. If there is no organization of self-defense corps after the Qingxiang is completed, it will not be sufficient to consolidate the people's self-defense foundation, and the previous efforts will inevitably be in vain, and the people will still not be able to live and work in peace permanently. The Qingxiang affairs in various counties are mostly scheduled to end at the end of March. It is urgent to quickly organize the self-defense corps in various districts according to law. The districts that have already been organized should also be inspected and reorganized to ensure that the entire effort is completed and permanent peace is maintained. Yesterday, instructions were issued to the Qingxiang Bureaus of various counties to list the organization and reorganization situations in detail and report them to the department for verification.

The Chamber of Commerce Supervisory Committee May Not Establish a Chairman: The Jiangsu Provincial Party Affairs Reorganization Committee previously inquired whether the county chamber of commerce supervisory committee could establish standing committee members or a chairman, as there were no explicit regulations on this matter. Yesterday, it received a reply from the Training Department of the Central Executive Committee, stating that according to the regulations in Article 21 of the Chamber of Commerce Law and its implementation rules, the chamber of commerce supervisory committee should only temporarily elect one person as chairman when meeting. At times other than meetings, there is no need to establish one. After receiving the letter, the Provincial Party Affairs Reorganization Committee, in addition to sending a letter to the provincial government, has instructed the party departments of various counties to notify them for their information. Conduct Cooperation Business Lectures. The Zhenjiang County Government, in order to promote cooperative businesses, enable members of various societies to clearly understand the meaning of cooperation, and promote rural business cooperation, has specifically scheduled a Zhenjiang County Cooperative Business Lecture Conference at the Provincial Agricultural and Mining Products Exhibition Hall on April 21st and 22nd. In addition to speeches by Provincial Government Chairman Ye and Agricultural Department Director He, cooperative experts Tang Qiyu and Tong Yumin will also be invited to give lectures.

Chongming

Large-Scale Joint Suppression of Bandits by Army, Navy, and Police: In recent years, the counties of Tong, Ru, Chong, and Hai have been plagued by bandits, and robbery cases have sprung up, causing the people to suffer deeply. The work of suppressing bandits is indeed urgent. It is heard that the provincial government has instructed the Coastal Patrol Office of the entire province and the Fourth Water Police District to quickly dispatch large detachments of army and navy, as well as two aircraft, to thoroughly suppress the bandit troubles in the counties of Tong, Ru, Chong, and Hai, and has designated Gong Mianqin, the captain of the 17th Water Police Team stationed in Chongming, as the commander of the bandit suppression operation, and decided to strictly encircle and suppress the bandit strongholds in counties such as Lügao and Qidong, in order to completely resolve the problem. It is heard that the Naval Patrol Office has dispatched four warships. After receiving the order a few days ago, Captain Gong also led the team headquarters under his jurisdiction, as well as the Pingyang, Jinghai, and Jingdong warships, to Jiangbei to jointly suppress the bandits.

Nantong

Building a Motor Road Along the Coast of Northern Jiangsu: The coastline of Northern Jiangsu, from Lüsi Port to Yancheng, extends for more than six hundred li. Due to inconvenient transportation, sea bandits lie in wait, making it difficult for the army to suppress them. Recently, the military and political authorities have agreed to allocate pacification troops to use the original Fan Dike to expand and build a motor road. Once the engineering team is organized, work will begin immediately.

Sea Bandits Scattered from Lüsi: Sea bandits causing trouble in the Lüsi area are now scattered by boat due to official suppression. There are still bandit boats drifting on the ocean surface, listening for land movements.

Rugao

Four Criminals Handed Over to the County Court for Handling: The Lugang Self-Defense Corps of the 16th District arrested three criminals, Tang Yucai, Chang Xinbao, and Xiao Wenlou, at Guqi Luzhuang Majia, etc., the day before yesterday. They confessed to being bandits. Yesterday, they were sent to the county court with official documents for handling. In addition, the Self-Defense Corps of the 14th District arrested a criminal, Fan Wen, the day before yesterday and also handed him over to the county for handling yesterday.

An Elderly Woman in Her Sixties Was Burned to Death: Li Shishi, a female villager in Huangzhen Yang Shiqing's village, aged about sixty, was burned to death by Gu Shunpei of Tongjiafen with large grass and firewood on the night of the 5th of this month for unknown reasons. The district public office in that area has arrested Gu and sent him to the county government for investigation and requested that someone be sent to inspect the scene.

Hangzhou

The Third Lottery Draw for Construction Bonds: The third redemption lottery for Zhejiang construction bonds was held at the City Chamber of Commerce this afternoon (the 15th). Representatives from various agencies were dispatched to supervise. At about 2 o'clock, Tang Shijian was sent by the Finance Department to the meeting to conduct the lottery in groups according to regulations and reported that the redemption this time was 400,000 yuan and the interest payment was more than 360,000 yuan. Also, the Bond Fund Management Committee has been established. Please have the committee representative report the amount of income. The representative reported that the total income from November of last year to April 14th was 768,000 yuan, all of which was deposited in the Central, China, Local, Agricultural, and Industrial Four Banks. This redemption and interest payment will be issued by the four banks and the county governments based on the bonds starting from the 30th of this month. Then, the lottery was divided into four groups, and the extracted numbers were 09, 38, 65, and 96. Regardless of the denominations of 1,000 yuan, 100 yuan, or 10 yuan, those bonds whose last two digits are the same as the extracted numbers have won the lottery.

Taizhou

Major Fire at Qiansuo: A fire suddenly broke out at the Tang family in Qiansuo, north of Linhai, at one o'clock last night. The fire was so intense that it could not be extinguished for an hour, destroying more than a dozen houses and causing losses of about 2,000 yuan. Reassignment of the Luqiao Public Security Branch Director: Hu Shuxing, director of the Luqiao Public Security Branch in Huangyan, has been reassigned, and Yin Zhenzhong has been appointed to fill the vacancy. He has already taken office.

Letter from the Huai River Conservancy Commission 12

Having recently read the news article on the 13th of this month in your newspaper regarding the use of the Huai River Conservancy Commission's Boxer Indemnity funds, much of the content does not match the facts. During the meeting held by this commission on March 11, Committee Member Li Yishe did propose this motion, but after discussion, it was generally believed that the Boxer Indemnity funds were still pending, and the case should be reserved for further discussion. The principle was not approved, nor was it resolved that "the matter would be handled immediately after the Boxer Indemnity funds are allocated." The interest was not mentioned at all. Fearing that the rumors are untrue and would cause misunderstandings, please investigate and publish this entire letter to correct the record. Secretariat of the Huai River Conservancy Commission, April 14.

Education News

Important News

Ministry of Education Investigates the Number of Overseas Students 13

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education sent two types of survey forms (A and B) for Chinese students to various embassies abroad, requesting them to fill them out locally in order to compile statistics on overseas students. The original letter stated, "We are currently in the process of compiling statistics on Chinese students studying abroad and have formulated two types of survey forms, A and B. Form B has been sent to your embassy with a request to fill it out. However, the countries are vast and the students are scattered everywhere. Relying solely on the embassy's direct handling may not be sufficient. Moreover, Form B only surveys students who have not returned to China. As for those who have returned to China and those who have been studying abroad for many years, it is extremely difficult to investigate due to the political changes and the scattering of documents in the country. Therefore, we have specifically formulated an English survey form and plan to forward it to various schools above the specialty level in your country of residence for their consideration and filling out in order to ensure accuracy and avoid omissions. In addition to sending separate letters, we are enclosing the forms for your investigation and forwarding, and we request that they be filled out and returned. Sincerely, to various embassies abroad."

Jiangsu Education Department Order 14

Report Private Primary Schools That Have Not Been Registered

The Jiangsu Provincial Education Department ordered the education bureaus of various counties, stating, "According to the regulations of the Ministry of Education on the registration of private primary schools, county education bureaus shall approve the registration of elementary primary schools and report it to the Education Department for record-keeping. The Education Department shall approve the registration of complete primary schools, which has already been notified for compliance. At present, there are quite a few private primary schools in various counties that have applied for registration, but there are still some who delay reporting or intentionally evade it. If we do not conduct a careful assessment, we will not only violate the law, but also mislead children and cause harm. In addition to issuing separate orders, we are hereby instructing your director to comply with the order and quickly submit a list of private primary schools that have been approved for registration before this year. Those that have not been registered should also submit a detailed list for examination. You should also instruct them to quickly proceed with the registration in accordance with the prescribed procedures. Violators will be severely punished. You must comply with this order separately and report back within one month. This order is urgent."

Wang Maozu Gave a Lecture on Education Policy 17

Gave a Speech at Shanghai High School Yesterday and Will Go to Wuxi Today

Mr. Wang Maozu, the principal of Suzhou Middle School, has been serving in education for more than ten years and has made great contributions to education in our country. He came to Shanghai yesterday to give a lecture on education policy at Shanghai High School. The audience was very satisfied. The following is a brief summary of his lecture:

I. The constitution or constitution should be based on the educational purpose of the Republic of China and Article 13 of the domestic policy of the Kuomintang platform to compile a special chapter on education.

II. Education funds in each province and county must be guaranteed independently, then reorganized and increased, and the nature of tax revenue should be assessed and the proportion of various educational uses should be allocated. For tax revenues with universality, where the poor and the rich share equally, such as the salt surcharge tax, most of it should be used for compulsory education, mass education, and primary vocational schools.

III. Livelihood education advocates breaking the habit of schools and changing to production-oriented vocational education. For example, agricultural farms are currently being established in various counties. Primary agricultural schools should be established on the farms. Provincial factories should seek to be restored, and model factories should be established in various counties, and industrial training classes should be established in the factories.

IV. Teacher training is the basis for promoting compulsory education. If the current quality and quantity cannot be taken care of economically and time-wise, the quantity should be expanded first, methods should be found to encourage it, and the length of service should be stipulated, and annual seniority increases should be implemented.

V. Secondary education: junior high school focuses on universality, and senior high school focuses on selection and concentration. A four-three system is adopted, or students are separately admitted to higher education and employment. The curriculum for students entering higher education is consistent for six years, while the curriculum for employment is four years.

VI. Quickly determine the amount of scholarships for poor students so that students who are poor and hardworking can enter higher education without being restricted by economics.

VII. Higher education: National universities should be enriched, provincial universities should not be established, and private universities should be rewarded and subsidized and restrained at the same time. Universities should be established in Mongolia and Tibet to recruit students from inland, give them awards, and stipulate service regulations in order to develop frontier undertakings and develop culture. Specialized schools should be established more and cooperate with large factories, such as paper mills can open paper-making specialty schools, which should be rewarded by the state.

VIII. Overseas Chinese education is not worried about lack of money, but about lack of talent. A training class for overseas Chinese teachers should be established in the Fujian and Guangdong normal schools, courses for studying the life problems of overseas Chinese should be added, and local diplomatic personnel should be evaluated for their efforts in education.

IX. Establish a compilation and translation museum under the Central Research Institute, reward writings, and X. Guarantee educational personnel, stipulate examination methods, and implement annual seniority salary increases and pension system. It is heard that Mr. Wang has also accepted the invitation of President Gao of Wuxi Education College and will go to Wuxi to give a lecture on mass education.

Sino-Western 18

Charity Football Match

丨This Sunday at the China Baseball Field丨

Lineups Determined

The Shanghai Charity Football Match, sponsored by the China National Sports Federation, is scheduled to take place this Sunday (the 19th) at 3 PM at the China Baseball Field. As the football season is about to end, this grand and charitable Sino-Western match serves as a fitting finale, which is worthy of our anticipation.

The Chinese Team's Lineup

The Chinese team's lineup has not yet been officially announced. However, according to our sources, it has been internally decided that it will be the same Chinese team that won this year's All-China Football Championship. It is possible that some adjustments may be necessary due to player availability. For example, Luo Haiguang, the left inside forward, previously played for the East China team and was hospitalized for treatment after an injury. Although he has recovered without medication, it is uncertain whether he will still be able to play for China. However, Chen Hongguang has recovered well and can easily take his place. The most difficult point is the central player of the Chinese team. Chen Zhenhe is certainly a suitable candidate, but he is also a crucial forward and it is difficult to move him. Zhuang Shihong has not fully recovered from his injuries, so how can he be asked to play again? Li Ning is not familiar with the position, so how can he be forced into it? Therefore, we can only rely on Feng Yunyou. Chen Jiaqiu is better as a right outside forward than a right inside forward. If the "two Guangs" (Luo Haiguang and Chen Hongguang) play side by side, then Chen Jiaqiu will be able to showcase his skills. The following lineup is the best we can offer and will surely bring us good results:

Zhou Xianyan, Li Ning, Jiang Shanqing, Chen Pu, Feng Yunyou, Chen Jiaqiu, Chen Zhenhe

The Western Customs Team's Lineup

The Western Customs team, having won the three major championships this year, has agreed to be one of the main attractions of this year's Sino-Western charity match. The lineup has also been revealed. According to experts, the team's overall talent is outstanding. A detailed introduction is provided below for the reference of the Chinese athletes. As the saying goes, "Know yourself and know your enemy, and you will win every battle." The goalkeeper is named Blatley. His talent is slightly inferior to Zhou Xianyan, but he is considered a giant among Westerners. Gerbertson and Scott will play as the left and right fullbacks. In recent matches, they have given us the impression of being "solid and reliable." The center back line of Whis Ujal Shucheden is the strongest point of the team. Their undefeated record this season is due to this line. The forwards, Okeley, Jack, Farlas, Turner, and Wilkinson, are known as the "Five Tigers of the Sea." They are strong and have powerful shots. When we meet them, we will know their skills.

Blatley, Scott, Gerbertson, Hrey Ujal, Shucheden Whis, Wilkinson, Turner, Farlas, Jack, Okeley

Malayan Overseas Chinese Sports Meet (1) 26

Grand Opening Ceremony - The Great Undertaking of the Overseas Chinese

丨700 Athletes Participating丨Over 10,000 Spectators丨

President Hu Wenhu Delivers Opening Address, Consul General Chen Delivers Speech

丨Men's 100-Meter Preliminary Round Breaks National Record丨

(Singapore Correspondence, April 3) The Malayan Overseas Chinese Sports Meet, which has been in preparation for years, finally opened grandly at the Jalan Besar Stadium today at 10 AM, amidst the enthusiastic support of over 10,000 people. With months of painstaking effort, today's excellent results have been achieved, which can be said to be worthy of this undertaking. It will be seen that a brilliant flower will be opened widely in the history of sports in the South Seas, and the national spirit will also be further stimulated. Therefore, today's grand event cannot be said to be unimportant. The circumstances before and after the opening of the conference are described in sections below.

The Rain Suddenly Clears

The weather in the South Seas is often unpredictable. It can be sunny one moment and rainy and windy the next. This is a common occurrence for those who have lived here for a long time. Before 8 AM this morning, it suddenly rained heavily. The general audience was worried, as if the weather did not cooperate, this solemn opening ceremony might be suspended, which would be cause for concern.

Beautiful Venue Layout

Outside the venue, the words "Malayan Overseas Chinese Sports Meet" were written in large characters. Above, the emblems of China and England were hung high. In the southeast corner of the venue, a platform was set up. Behind the platform, a white cloth was used as a screen, respectfully displaying a portrait of Sun Yat-sen. The portrait was surrounded by beautiful and eye-catching colorful flowers and crossed national flags. On both sides of the platform, two tables were placed, on which were placed prizes from important figures and celebrities at home and abroad. The door of the platform and the surrounding area were decorated with green leaves. On the upper left corner of the platform, a loudspeaker was placed for issuing commands. The venue was filled with national flags, especially the national flag of our country. Small flags with slogans such as "The world is for all under the Great Way," "The Three Principles of the People," "Long Live the Republic of China," and "Support the Party and the Nation" were also hung every three to five small flags.

Lively Opening Ceremony

There were about 10,000 Chinese and Western spectators, as well as teachers and students from various schools. Around 8 AM, athletes from various districts, such as Singapore, Penang, Selangor, Johor, and others, successively entered the venue in orderly formations, with organized steps. Some sang school songs, while others sang party songs. The sound was loud, almost stopping the clouds. The athletes from each team were full of energy. The first team was the entire staff of the Malayan Overseas Chinese Sports Meet, the second team was the athletes from the Selangor district, the third team was the athletes from the Perak district, the fourth team was the athletes from the Penang district, the fifth team was the athletes from the Negeri Sembilan district, and the sixth team was the athletes from the Singapore district. The opening ceremony was held at 9 AM. The Yangzheng Military Band led the way, circling the venue. Each team had a school flag and a national flag as its guide. In front of the military band was the conference flag and the national flag. Afterwards, students from various schools marched around the stadium in lines of four, winding like a snake on Changshan Mountain. For a time, the sound of military music, whistles, and footsteps echoed each other, creating a solemn atmosphere. When the order was given to raise the flag in the fourth item, the athletes and spectators in each district applauded thunderously. The order of the ceremony and the speeches are listed on the left.

Order of the Opening Ceremony

(1) Music (Yangzheng Brass Band) (2) All Staff, Athletes, Group Gymnastics, Students Marching around the Venue (3) Take Seats (4) Everyone Stands at Attention (5) Raise the Flag (Music) (6) Sing the National Anthem (Music) (7) Bow Three Times to the National Flag, the Party Flag, and the Portrait of Sun Yat-sen (8) Respectfully Read Sun Yat-sen's Will (9) Three Minutes of Silence (10) President Delivers Opening Address (11) Athlete Oath Ceremony (12) Consul General Chen Delivers Speech (13) Vice President Delivers Speech (14) Chief of Preparations Reports on the Preparation Process (15) Speech (16) Sing the Sports Meet Song (17) Shout Slogans (18) Photography (19) Music (20) Thousand-Person Gymnastics Performance (Ying Xin School, Qi Deng School, Industrial and Commercial School, Women's Sports Academy, Hequn Yixue, Nanyang Girls' School, Yangzheng School, Overseas Chinese Civilian School, Nanyang Civilian School, Junyuan School, Dan Zhao School, Lixin School, Shuren School, Yuying School)

Consul General Chen's Speech

In brief, he said, "Today is the opening ceremony of the Malayan Overseas Chinese Sports Meet. Athletes from various districts of Malaya have gathered here to compete in sports, to promote and increase their physical and mental health. It is a grand and unprecedented event. I am very honored to be able to participate in this grand event. I hope that the athletes from various districts will show their spirit and strive to achieve the goal of participating in this event and winning. I hope that the athletes from various districts will strictly abide by the order of the entire venue. Every competition should be regarded as a friendly competition. All actions should be for the glory of the team and for the honor of our nation."

Report on the Preparation Process

Chief of Preparations Lin Jindian said in general, "Today is the day of the Malayan Conference. I am honored to be able to attend this grand event. Looking back on the initiation of the conference, it was actually in early May of last year. Two weeks later, the initiating meeting drafted the program, and two weeks later, the chairman and vice-chairman were elected, and the heads of each department were appointed. On June 14th, the Preparations Office was established. I was mistakenly elected by the public as the director of the Preparations Office in October. Thanks to the support of my colleagues, I have worked hard and dared not slacken. Fortunately, each district pre-selected and successively held events, and the conference was able to be opened. This is not the work of the Preparations Office staff, but the performance of the enthusiasm of the entire overseas Chinese community for sports. Since the establishment of the Preparations Office, we have worked hard on publicity, but due to limited capabilities, the publicity was not thorough, and a few overseas Chinese were unable to send representatives, which is very regrettable. I hope that next year, when the Chinese Conference is held elsewhere, all Malayan overseas Chinese will have representatives to participate. As for the expenses of the Preparations Office, in addition to the donations from me and Hu Wenbao, totaling 3,000 yuan, Hu Wenhu temporarily filled out 5,000 yuan and did not solicit any donations from the outside world. Now that the conference is hastily opened, the preparations are not complete, and I hope that the athletes from various districts will forgive me, and I hope that everyone will work together in each spirit to make this conference a complete success. Time is short, so I will give this simple report."

Hu Wenhu's Opening Address

The President of the Conference, Hu Wenhu, delivered the opening address, saying, "The initiation of the Malayan Overseas Chinese Sports Meet has been going on for ten months. Thanks to the hard work of the staff of the Preparations Office and the sincere cooperation of sports enthusiasts in various districts, today we have this solemn opening ceremony, with thousands of men and women from eight districts working together to compete without contention. Sports leaders from all over Malaya are guiding us to develop sports among the people and promote the spirit of the nation. It is truly an unprecedented event in Malaya. The significance of sports lies in improving the lives of human beings. Organized training has methods. Every action must be in accordance with the rules. We must strive to make it scientific. The manners and postures must strive to be beautiful. The speed and slowness of running must strive to be flexible. We must strive to make it artistic. A small skill can be perfected over time. The way to success is to be persistent and tireless, so as to cultivate a firm and diligent character. Forming teams and working together is a joint effort. The loss of one person can affect the whole situation, so as to cultivate the habit of teamwork. In the arena, referees are publicly elected, and orders and resolutions must be respected and obeyed, so as to cultivate the spirit of obedience to discipline. From this point of view, the purpose of promoting sports is not to train a group of violent and reckless people who are good at fighting, but to seek the balanced development of virtue, intelligence, physical fitness, and aesthetics, and to cultivate a great personality. The more overseas Chinese are abroad, the further away they are from their homeland, the criticisms of being 'sick men' and 'loose sand' are constantly heard, and the improper habits and irregular lifestyles are destroying their race and causing shame to the country. The opening of the conference will make the atmosphere of sports permeate the South Seas. The morale will be boosted, and the spirit will be multiplied. When the entire overseas Chinese community hears about it, the stubborn and cowardly will have the ambition to stand up. It is not shallow that it is beneficial to the people and the country. I am not talented, but I am fortunate to attend this grand event. I respectfully offer my humble words to express my sincerity. Although the words are limited, the meaning is endless. I, my elders, brothers, sisters, please remember it." The Vice President of the Conference, Liang Xinnan, delivered a speech, saying in brief, "Today, the Malayan Overseas Chinese will hold the opening ceremony here. Athletes from all over Malaya are participating, so that this unprecedented conference will be successful. This is due to the strong promotion and sacrifice of the Preparations Committee members and the enthusiastic overseas Chinese in various places. Without the spirit of time, today's grand occasion could not have been achieved. In recent years, the progress of our British overseas Chinese in sports and the expression of the spirit of the nation have been advancing by leaps and bounds. I hope that the athletes from various districts will work hard and live up to the enthusiasm of the overseas Chinese in various places in promoting this Malayan Overseas Chinese Sports Meet, and establish a permanent and strong foundation for our Chinese nation." (Applause) Another Vice President of the Conference, Zhang Kaichuan, delivered a speech.

Everyone Shouted Slogans

Promote sports among the people, unite the will of the entire overseas Chinese community, express the spirit of the nation, long live the Malayan Overseas Chinese Sports Meet, long live the Republic of China!

Men's 100-Meter Preliminary Round

There were a total of four groups in the men's 100-meter preliminary round. The first place in the second and fourth groups had very good scores, all 11 seconds. If officially approved, it would be equal to Huang Bingkun's national 100-meter record of 11 seconds.

Group Number

Zou Zuohua Set Sail Yesterday 27

Inspection Period Scheduled for One Year

Newly Appointed to the Rank of General

Zou Zuohua, the commissioner for land reclamation in the Xing'an region, was ordered by Zhang Xueliang to go to Europe and America to inspect land reclamation projects. Xu Kechang, deputy section chief of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, was also transferred to assist him. Zou and his party took a ferry prepared by the China Flag Shipping Company at the New Customs Wharf yesterday morning at around 10 AM, and went directly to the Dalae Wharf in Pudong to board the Adam President, a ship of the Dalae Company, to set sail. The ship set anchor at 12:30 PM yesterday. Those who went to the New Customs Wharf to see him off included Tang Liu and his wife, the director of the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Song Menghu, the secretary of the land reclamation commissioner's office in the Xing'an region, and Liu, the director of the agricultural affairs section, among others. In addition to Xu Kechang, Zou was also accompanied by a German female secretary. According to Zou, he told our reporter yesterday that he planned to go to France first, then to England, Germany, Austria, Italy, and other countries to conduct inspections. Finally, he would go to the United States. The trip is expected to take one year. The travel expenses are entirely provided by Vice Commander Zhang. Mr. Song Menghu also plans to go with him, but because the affairs of the land reclamation office have not been completed, he still needs to return to the Xing'an region to take care of them. In the future, he will transfer to Europe from Siberia. Furthermore, it is reported that Zou received an order from the central government the day before yesterday, promoting him to the rank of general.
